msg:The environment around the hotel is quiet and pleasant, away from the hustle and bustle of the crowd. Moreover, this hotel is very new, and the lobby design is super bright. As soon as you enter, there is a faint fragrance, and you feel relaxed.

The room is much larger than other hotels of the same level, and the floor height is very high, and the space feels bigger. The layout is also simple and generous, and it still has its own characteristics. Especially the dark green marble countertop, under the light and shadow, it looks as mysterious and deep as in the sea. The window frame also has a slightly irregular design, which reminds me of the bubbles in the sea. In short, if you look closely at the small details of the room, many places echo the elements of the sea. It can be said that the designer team is very attentive.

The service is really as other reviews say, it's really good! Whether it's the front desk reception or the room service, or even the friends at the concierge, they are always smiling and can sense our needs in advance. For example, we checked in a little early and the room was not ready, but the little brother took the initiative to upgrade our room so that we could check in immediately. When we left, a staff member saw that we paused for a while, and immediately came forward to ask, and took the initiative to help us push the box, and took us to the elevator.

In terms of sea view, the hotel in Golden Beach is better, but in other aspects, Westin is perfect. (But to be honest, Marriott's superior sea view room only has half a window to see the sea view. This half-wall and half-window prison experience is better off without sea view.)

The buffet is useless, the hairy crabs have been steamed, and the legs have fallen off, some are still dead, not very fresh and have a strange smell. Shrimp and sashimi are fresh. The eel with foie gras is very good, and the price is quite a bargain.

It was already dirty and covered with paper as a new slipper and put it in the slipper compar**ent. This is very speechless.

3. The service is OK. The overall service attitude is very professional, polite, and full of kindness to the children. For example, the lady in the lobby will offer candies to coax the children when they are unhappy. The manager on duty at check-in saw the children and brought an air purifier to our room.

The fly in the oin**ent is that it is a bit far away from some Internet celebrity attractions. Now that the peak tourist season has passed, the road is still a bit congested, so it will take more time on the road. PS Yantai is like Yangma Island and Long Island, which is worth visiting with your parents and children. Other places are somewhat boring.
